🚩 8 AM ➜ 🏁 11:30 AM 🌥 55f ➜ ☀ 68f 🚴🏻 37.49 mi 🚵🏻 517 ft 🅿️ Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ☕ Sweet Elle Cafe 328 11th St, Huntington Beach, CA 92648 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

27
JUL
周日
往西，越过天际(Skyline)吧骚年

路线: Redwood Townhall 集合 - OLH 爬坡 - Loma 邱林 - Pescadero 小镇 - San Gregorio 小店 - Tunitas 爬坡 - Kings Mountain 下山 适合夏天的避暑路线 credit @Steve 有两个大爬坡，分别是大家熟悉的 Old La Honda，和很多人熟悉的从Bike Hut开始的Tunitas Creek Rd 预计总时间6 hours 本路线也叫避暑路线，因为在树林中穿行，或是海边吹风。起始从Redwood Townhall出发，这也是在 [旧金山湾区骑行路线 第一章 练]( 介绍过的OLH老本田训练路线的起始点，可以把这个地方看作是湾区骑行的一个hub，因为很多骑行路线无论是转山还是休闲骑还是辣堡团，都会以这里为起点或者经过这里。 这一路上有很多可以驻足休息的好玩的地方，像Pescadero小镇和San Gregorio小店，还有下图的 The Bike Hut。一路的风景也有很多令我初见惊艳的地方。期待您也去探索一番，发现不一样的景色。

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Saturday Ride

Hi everyone, This Saturday, we will head up Metcalf Rd. via the Leyland Park maze to McKean. We will stop at the Calero parking lot on McKean for bathroom/water before descending Bailey and heading up Metcalf. There is also a bathroom and water fountain at the top of Metcalf. After the climb, we will descend San Felipe Rd before heading up IBM and back to Los Gatos. The route is 55 miles and about 4,700 ft of elevation gain. Wheels roll from Mike's Bikes at 8:35am sharp.

4B4NB5 🚩 8 AM ➜ 🏁 11:30 AM ☀ 52f ➜ ☀ 66f 🚴🏻 37.64 mi 🚵🏻 1,020 ft 🅿️ Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ☕ Chaupain Bakery 2622 San Miguel Dr, Newport Beach, CA 92660 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

🚩 8 AM ➜ 🏁 11:30 AM 🌥 49f ➜ ☀ 55f 🚴🏻 37.56 mi 🚵🏻 1,832 ft 🅿️ Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 ☕️ Brown Sugar 26851 Aliso Creek Rd, Aliso Viejo, CA 92656 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Road Ride: Quimby (Saturday, Jan 25; Hammer pace)

This Saturday we wind our way toward Quimby, the funnest way to reach the first junction of the Mt. Hamilton climb. There’s a rest stop just up the road where we’ll regroup. If you want to use this as a launch pad for a Mt. Hamilton climb, please feel free, but the official ride descends back into the valley through rolling hills, returning to Los Gatos. Newcomers are welcome, but expect a swift pace. Don’t hesitate to reach out to me if you want to give it a shot but would like an escape option. —Dan

周一
LGBRC MLK Day Bonus Monday Road Ride

Hi team, I am planning to lead a bonus ride for this Monday, January 20th. The ride will head up Hicks Rd from the north before stopping for a regroup (bathroom and water rest) at the Almaden Quicksilver parking lot. From there, we will paceline from McKean Rd along Uvas before turning left on Willow Springs and heading back to Los Gatos via Santa Teresa and IBM. The route is 54.5 miles with 3700 ft of elevation gain. Wheels roll at 8:35 am sharp. This is a no drop ride. I hope to see you there!

Group road Ride - IBM from Santa Teresa Park Side

Please note this is the SUNDAY ride, starting from Mike's Bikes in Los Gatos. Wheels roll at 8:30. Route will head out Shannon and follow Coleman till we pass Almaden Lake Park and turn right into the neighborhoods. At mile 13 we visit Bernal-Gulnac-Joice Ranch with water/bathroom. At mile 16 we summit the north side of IBM, stopping for a quick regroup before descending the south side and heading back to Mike's Bikes. Route is 30 miles with 1,800 feet of climbing.

🚩 8 AM ➜ 🏁 11:30 AM ⛅️ 47f ➜ 🌤️ 58f 🚴🏻 39.59 mi 🚵🏻 448 ft 🅿️ Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ☕ Portfolio Fit 4101 E Olympic Plaza, Long Beach, CA 90803 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LGBRC Saturday Road Ride OLH via Arastradero/Alpine

Hi team, This Saturday, I will lead the group to Old La Honda road in Woodside. We will meet at Mike’s Bikes in Los Gatos at 8:30 AM, wheels will roll at 8:35 AM. We will head to Old La Honda road in a counter-clockwise direction, beginning by taking Hwy9 to Pierce, followed by climbing Mt. Eden and descending down to Steven’s Canyon. We will try to keep the group together by paceline on Foothill, before turning on Arastradero Rd. We will stop for water/bathroom on Arastradero Rd before heading a bit further west into Portola Valley. We will regroup at the top of OLH before beginning our ride back to Los Gatos via Skyline and Hwy9. I will strongly advocate for keeping the group together as much as possible on Skyline Blvd. If needed, we can also stop for bathroom/water at the Skyline and Page Mill intersection. The ride is 54 miles with just over 5000ft of elevation gain. Please bring plenty of nutrition and water and remember to refuel and rehydrate throughout the ride.

SF3UN8 Roll out: 8 AM Coffee break: 30-40 minutes ETA back: 11:30AM ☀ 49f ➜ ☀ 64f Distance: ⭐️⭐️ Elevation: ⭐️ 🅿️ Pico Rivera Golf Club 3260 Fairway Dr, Pico Rivera, CA 90660 ☕️ Delight Pastry (16.84M) 39 N Raymond Ave, Pasadena, CA 91103 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

9Q6WS4 Roll out: 8 AM Coffee break: 30-40 minutes ETA back: 11:20AM 🌥 51f ➜ 🌤 62f Distance: ⭐️⭐️ Elevation: 🅿️ Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 ☕ The Vintage 1979 9252 Garden Grove Blvd Unit 28 and 27, Garden Grove, CA 92844 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] Saturday Road Ride on December 28th

Dear fellow teammates, Forecast looks promising for this Saturday and perfect for a nice endurance adventure. The plan is to climb Mt Tam and ride along the coast for some scenic views. As always we will be regrouping on top of the main climbs and at the bottom of the technical descents. If you are planning on joining I would ask if you could please RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride. Please notice that the route may be subject to changes as we are still refining it 😊

LGBRC Saturday Portola Valley Loop

Hi team, For those who would prefer to stay local on Saturday, we will head to Portola Valley from Los Gatos via Pierce/Mt. Eden before pacelining up Foothill to Sand Hill Rd. I plan to stop for restroom/water at the Mt. Eden/Steven's Creek intersection (not shown on map) and in Portola Valley (shown on map). Rain cancels the ride, but the forecast looks promising. Wheels roll at 8:35 am.

[LGBRC Rides] Sunday Gravel Ride on December 22nd

Dear fellow teammates, Notice that this is a parallel ride to the regular Sunday road ride offered by the club. Plan is to do a long gravel ride along two iconic parks: Calero and QuickSilver. The ride will be a bit demanding, so please do not forget to bring lots of food and water. Also notice that this ride may be cancelled in case of rain or wet terrain. As always we will be regrouping on top of the main climbs and at the bottom of the technical descent. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

时间: 8:30 AM, Sunday, DEC 22, 2024

Sunday Road Ride - Calero Park

We do some nice warmup climbs and wind through the Leyland Park maze before embarking on the feature, the classic McKean Rd TT out to Calero Park, where there are restrooms and water. McKean can be a hammer fest when certain instigators (such as me) show up, but the focus this week is on collaboration and teamwork. I promise!

Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

Saturday Road Ride - Cañada, West OLH, Skyline Loop

We made it to the end of the year. I’m looking forward to some mellow team riding after a few months of sprinty cyclocross. Lots of paceline on the way out along Foothill and through Portola valley. First rest stop is at town hall on Portola Rd. Then onto Cañada and up 92 to Skyline. A bunch of climbing, then a right turn to partially descend La Honda. Be vigilant here, as we’ll be making a tricky left turn onto West Old La Honda to get back up to Skyline. Then we stay the course until Page Mill where we can take a rest room stop, then a quick water refill if needed at the fire station and finally down 9 and back to home base.

LGBRC Sunday Ride

发起人: Rachel Vasquez

活动来源: Strava Club - Los Gatos Bicycle Racing Club

周日
2024
Endurance Training Ride

The proposed route is Mt Hamilton all the way out to Patterson and back. Depending on how the group feels and the weather we can assess fatigue at the top of Hamilton, and at The Junction before heading all the way into Patterson. The target pace is to finish in 8-10hrs. This is a strict no-drop ride as the route is very remote and the riders should stick together to support one another in the event of a crash or severe mechanical. With that said, if you struggle to get up Hamilton in 2.5hrs I may ask you to turn back as it will be hard to finish the ride in the time window. Be self-sufficient with navigation, basic repair supplies, food, and water. There’s water at the top of Hamilton and at The Junction. The ride will definitely finish after dark so have lights to descend Hamilton. Feel free to DM me on strava or the club WhatsApp for further details. Wheels roll at 8am

时间: 8:00 AM, Sunday, DEC 15, 2024

集合GPS: 37.38404, -121.81597

R8WQ5F 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ☀ 52f ➜ ☀ 65f Distance: ⭐️⭐️ Elevation: ⭐️ 🅿️ Via Verde Park & Ride 105 Via Verde Dr Rd, San Dimas, CA 91773 ☕️ Iron & Kin Coffee Co (17.42M) 536 W 1st St, Claremont, CA 91711 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

LU2NQ2 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ☁ 48f ➜ ☁ 67f Distance: ⭐️⭐️ Elevation: 🅿️ Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 ☕️ Smoking Tiger Bread Factory (20.99M) 11900 South St #134, Cerritos, CA 90703 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

[LGBRC Rides] Saturday Road Ride on December 7th

Dear Fellow teammates, We have again a great forecast for this weekend apart from some colder temperatures. The plan for this Saturday is to paceline all together on a flatter route and head North. As always, we will stop and regroup to make sure the peloton stays together and we do not miss any important turns. As always, if you are planning on joining it would be great if you could RSVP on the Strava event, so that I can keep you updated on any changes of plan. Also feel free to contact me in private for more info or to coordinate the ride.

78VP6T 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes 🌥 57f ➜ 🌤 79f Distance: ⭐️⭐️ Elevation: 🅿️ Artic 2626 E Katella Ave, Anaheim, CA 92806 ☕️ Brew Story (22.43M) 16889 Beach Blvd, Huntington Beach, CA 92647 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

PP96KV 7:45 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes ☁ 55f ➜ 🌥 62f Distance: ⭐️⭐️ Elevation: ⭐️ 🅿️ Valencia High School 618 Bradford Ave, Placentia, CA 92870 ☕️ Phin Smith (18.24M) 12921 Main St, Garden Grove, CA 92840 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!

7:30 AM Roll out, and a coffee break for 30-40 minutes 🌥 52f ➜ 🌤 76f Distance: ⭐️⭐️ Elevation: ⭐️⭐️ 🅿️ Cypress Community Park 255 Visions, Irvine, CA 92620 ☕️ Oslo Coffee Co (21.23M) 25642 Crown Valley Pkwy Suite E1, Ladera Ranch, CA 92694 --------------------------------------------- **Sunday Group Ride Notice and Rules** Join us for our Sunday group ride! Here are the key details and rules to ensure a pleasant ride for everyone: 1. **Being On Time**: It is essential to BE ON TIME! We will start the ride sharp at the set time. 2. **No Drop Social Ride**: This ride is a no-drop, social ride. The main group will maintain a pace and there will be a few regroup points during the ride (e.g., before complicate route with multiple turns or after a long climb.) 3. ** Experience Level**: The pace will be comfortable for advance beginner with climbing experience. Ensure you have the necessary experience and fitness to participate. 4. **Group Ride Etiquette**: Familiarize yourself with basic group ride hand signals and unwritten ethics. 5. **Route Knowledge**: If you decide to ride at a faster pace and get separated from the group, know the route and be prepared to find your own way home. 6. **Newcomer Responsibility**: If you plan to bring friend(s), please ensure you download the map and stay with your friend(s), they are your responsibility. The main group will not delay the ride. 7. **Safety Gear**: Please bring a helmet, spare tubes, a pump or CO2 cartridges, water, and all necessary supplies. 8. **Participation Acknowledgment**: Participation in this event/ride is voluntary. Participants acknowledge the risks and/or dangers associated with cycling and are thus responsible for their own safety. We look forward to enjoyable ride. See you on the road!
